see if there is a fused-type version of function\n        # only valid for numeric\n        if callable(ftype):\n            f = ftype\n        else:\n            f = getattr(libgroupby, ftype)\n        if is_numeric:\n            return f\n        elif dtype == np.dtype(object):\n            if how in [\"median\", \"cumprod\"]:\n                # no fused types -> no __signatures__\n                raise NotImplementedError(\n                    f\"function is not implemented for this dtype: \"\n                    f\"[how->{how},dtype->{dtype_str}]\"\n                )\n            elif how in [\"std\", \"sem\", \"idxmin\", \"idxmax\"]:\n                # We have a partial object that does not have __signatures__\n                return f\n            elif how in [\"skew\", \"kurt\"]:\n                # _get_cython_vals will convert to float64\n                pass\n            elif \"object\" not in f.__signatures__:\n                # raise NotImplementedError here rather than TypeError later\n                raise NotImplementedError(\n                    f\"function is not implemented for this dtype: \"\n                    f\"[how->{how},dtype->{dtype_str}]\"\n                )\n            return f\n        else:\n            raise NotImplementedError(\n                \"This should not be reached. Please report a bug at \"\n                \"github.com/pandas-dev/pandas/\",\n                dtype,\n            )\n\n    def _get_cython_vals(self, values: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:\n        \"\"\"\n        Cast numeric dtypes to float64 for functions that only support that.\n\n        Parameters\n        ----------\n        values : np.ndarray\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        values : np.ndarray\n        \"\"\"\n        how = self.how\n\n        if how in [\"median\", \"std\", \"sem\", \"skew\", \"kurt\"]:\n            # median only has a float64 implementation\n            # We should only get here with is_numeric, as non-numeric cases\n            #  should raise in _get_cython_function\n            values = ensure_float64(values)\n\n        elif values.dtype.kind in \"iu\":\n            if how in [\"var\", \"mean\"] or (\n                self.kind == \"transform\" and self.has_dropped_na\n            ):\n                # Avoid overflow during group op\n                if values.dtype.kind == \"i\":\n                    values = ensure_int64(values)\n                else:\n                    values = ensure_uint64(values)\n\n        return values\n\n    def _get_output_shape(self, ngroups: int, values: np.ndarray) -> Shape:\n        how = self.how\n        kind = self.kind\n\n        arity = self._cython_arity.get(how, 1)\n\n        out_shape: Shape\n        if how == \"ohlc\":\n            out_shape = (ngroups, arity)\n        elif arity > 1:\n            raise NotImplementedError(\n                \"arity of more than 1 is not supported for the 'how' argument\"\n            )\n        elif kind == \"transform\":\n            out_shape = values.shape\n        else:\n            out_shape = (ngroups, *values.shape[1:])\n        return out_shape\n\n    def _get_out_dtype(self, dtype: np.dtype) -> np.dtype:\n        how = self.how\n\n        if how == \"rank\":\n            out_dtype = \"float64\"\n        elif how in [\"idxmin\", \"idxmax\"]:\n            # The Cython implementation only produces the row number; we'll take\n            # from the index using this in post processing\n            out_dtype = \"intp\"\n        elif dtype.kind in \"iufcb\":\n            out_dtype = f\"{dtype.kind}{dtype.itemsize}\"\n        else:\n            out_dtype = \"object\"\n        return np.dtype(out_dtype)\n\n    def _get_result_dtype(self, dtype: np.dtype) -> np.dtype:\n        \"\"\"\n        Get the desired dtype of a result based on the\n        input dtype and how it was computed.\n\n        Parameters\n        ----------\n        dtype : np.dtype\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        np.dtype\n            The desired dtype of the result.\n        \"\"\"\n        how = self.how\n\n        if how in [\"sum\", \"cumsum\", \"sum\", \"prod\", \"cumprod\"]:\n            if dtype == np.dtype(bool):\n                return np.dtype(np.int64)\n        elif how in [\"mean\", \"median\", \"var\", \"std\", \"sem\"]:\n            if dtype.kind in \"fc\":\n                return dtype\n            elif dtype.kind in \"iub\":\n                return np.dtype(np.float64)\n        return dtype\n\n    @final\n    def _cython_op_ndim_compat(\n        self,\n        values: np.ndarray,\n        *,\n        min_count: int,\n        ngroups: int,\n        comp_ids: np.ndarray,\n        mask: npt.NDArray[np.bool_] | None = None,\n        result_mask: npt.NDArray[np.bool_] | None = None,\n        initial: Any = 0,\n        **kwargs,\n    ) -> np.ndarray:\n        if values.ndim == 1:\n            # np.ndarray[ndim=2]\n        orig_values = values\n\n        dtype = values.dtype\n        is_numeric = dtype.kind in \"iufcb\"\n\n        is_datetimelike = dtype.kind in \"mM\"\n\n        if self.how in [\"any\", \"all\"]:\n            if mask is None:\n                mask = isna(values)\n\n        if is_datetimelike:\n            values = values.view(\"int64\")\n            is_numeric = True\n        elif dtype.kind == \"b\":\n            values = values.view(\"uint8\")\n        if values.dtype == \"float16\":\n            values = values.astype(np.float32)\n\n        if self.how in [\"any\", \"all\"]:\n            if dtype == object:\n                if kwargs[\"skipna\"]:\n                    # TODO: min_count\n            if self.how != \"rank\":\n                # TODO: should rank take result_mask?\n                kwargs[\"result_mask\"] = result_mask\n            func(\n                out=result,\n                values=values,\n                labels=comp_ids,\n                ngroups=ngroups,\n                is_datetimelike=is_datetimelike,\n                mask=mask,\n                **kwargs,\n            )\n\n        if self.kind == \"aggregate\" and self.how not in [\"idxmin\", \"idxmax\"]:\n            # i.e. counts is defined.  Locations where count<min_count\n            # need to have the result set to np.nan, which may require casting,\n            # see GH#40767. For idxmin/idxmax is handled specially via post-processing\n            if result.dtype.kind in \"iu\" and not is_datetimelike:\n                # if the op keeps the int dtypes, we have to use 0\n                cutoff = max(0 if self.how in [\"sum\", \"prod\"] else 1, min_count)\n                empty_groups = counts < cutoff\n                if empty_groups.any():\n                    if result_mask is not None:\n                        assert result_mask[empty_groups].all()\n                    else:\n                        # Note: this conversion could be lossy, see GH#40767\n                        result = result.astype(\"float64\")\n                        result[empty_groups] = np.nan\n\n        result = result.T\n\n        if self.how not in self.cast_blocklist:\n            # e.g. if we are int64 and need to restore to datetime64/timedelta64\n            # \"rank\" is the only member of cast_blocklist we get here\n            # Casting only needed for float16, bool, datetimelike,\n            #  and self.how in [\"sum\", \"prod\", \"ohlc\", \"cumprod\"]\n            res_dtype = self._get_result_dtype(orig_values.dtype)\n            op_result = maybe_downcast_to_dtype(result, res_dtype)\n        else:\n            op_result = result\n\n        return op_result\n\n    @final\n    def _validate_axis(self, axis: AxisInt, values: ArrayLike) -> \"\"\"\n        Groupby iterator\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        Generator yielding sequence of (name, subsetted object)\n        for each group\n        \"\"\"\n        splitter = @final\n    def _get_splitter(self, data: NDFrame) -> DataSplitter:\n        \"\"\"\n        Returns\n        -------\n        Generator yielding subsetted objects\n        \"\"\"\n        if data,\n            self.ngroups,\n            sorted_ids=self._sorted_ids,\n            sort_idx=self.result_ilocs,\n        )\n\n    @cache_readonly\n    def indices(self) -> dict[Hashable, npt.NDArray[np.intp]]:\n        \"\"\"dict {group name -> group indices}\"\"\"\n        if len(self.groupings) == 1 and isinstance(self.result_index, CategoricalIndex):\n            # This shows unused categories in indices GH#38642\n            result = self.groupings[0].indices\n        else:\n            codes_list = [ping.codes for ping in self.groupings]\n            result = @cache_readonly\n    def result_ilocs(self) -> npt.NDArray[np.intp]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Get the original integer locations of result_index in the input.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Original indices are where group_index would go via sorting.\n        # But when dropna is true, we need to remove null values while accounting for\n        # any gaps that then occur because of them.\n        ids = self.ids\n\n        if self.has_dropped_na:\n            mask = np.where(ids >= 0)\n            # Count how many gaps are caused by previous null values for each position\n            null_gaps = np.cumsum(ids == -1)[mask]\n            ids = ids[mask]\n\n        result = get_group_index_sorter(ids, self.ngroups)\n\n        if self.has_dropped_na:\n            # Shift by the number of prior null gaps\n            result += np.take(null_gaps, result)\n\n        return result\n\n    @property\n    def codes(self) -> list[npt.NDArray[np.signedinteger]]:\n        return [ping.codes for ping out: np.ndarray | list\n        if ngroups:\n            out = np.bincount(ids[ids != -1], minlength=ngroups)\n        else:\n            out = []\n        return Series(out, index=self.result_index, copy=False) for ping in self.groupings\n        ]\n        obs = [\n            ping._observed or not ping._passed_categorical for ping in self.groupings\n        ]\n        sorts = [ping._sort for ping in self.groupings]\n        # When passed a categorical grouping, keep all categories\n        for k, (ping, level) in enumerate(zip(self.groupings, levels, strict=True)):\n            if unobserved and observed parts\n            names = self.names\n            codes = [ping.codes for ping in self.groupings]\n            ob_indices = [idx for idx, ob in enumerate(obs) if ob]\n @cache_readonly\n    def result_ilocs(self) -> npt.NDArray[np.intp]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Get the original integer locations of result_index in the input.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Original OHLC\n\n    @classmethod\n    def get_kind_from_how(cls, how: str) -> str:\n        if how in cls._CYTHON_FUNCTIONS[\"aggregate\"]:\n            return \"aggregate\"\n        return \"transform\"\n\n    # Note: we make this a classmethod and pass kind+how so that caching\n    #  works at the class level and not the instance level\n    @classmethod\n    @functools.cache\n    def _get_cython_function(\n        cls, kind: str, how: str, dtype: np.dtype, is_numeric: bool\n    ):\n        dtype_str = dtype.name\n        ftype = cls._CYTHON_FUNCTIONS[kind][how]\n\n        # no fused types -> no __signatures__\n                raise NotImplementedError(\n                    f\"function is not implemented for this dtype: \"\n                    f\"[how->{how},dtype->{dtype_str}]\"\n                )\n            elif how in [\"std\", \"sem\", \"idxmin\", \"idxmax\"]:\n                # We have a partial object that does not have __signatures__\n                return f\n            elif how in [\"skew\", \"kurt\"]:\n                # _get_cython_vals will convert to float64\n                pass\n            elif \"object\" not in f.__signatures__:\n                # raise NotImplementedError here rather than TypeError later\n                raise NotImplementedError(\n                    f\"function is not implemented for this dtype: \"\n                    f\"[how->{how},dtype->{dtype_str}]\"\n                )\n            return f\n        else:\n            raise NotImplementedError(\n                \"This should not be reached. Please report a bug at \"\n                \"github.com/pandas-dev/pandas/\",\n                dtype,\n            )\n\n    def _get_cython_vals(self, values: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:\n        \"\"\"\n        Cast numeric dtypes to float64 for functions that only support that.\n\n        Parameters\n        ----------\n        values : np.ndarray\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        values : np.ndarray\n        \"\"\"\n        how = self.how\n\n        if how in [\"median\", \"std\", \"sem\", \"skew\", \"kurt\"]:\n            # median only has a float64 implementation\n            # We should only get here with is_numeric, as non-numeric cases\n            #  should raise in _get_cython_function\n            values = ensure_float64(values)\n\n        elif values.dtype.kind in \"iu\":\n            if how in [\"var\", \"mean\"] or (\n                self.kind == \"transform\" and self.has_dropped_na\n            ):\n                # has_dropped_na check need for test_null_group_str_transformer\n                # result may still include NaN, so we have to cast\n                values = ensure_float64(values)\n\n            elif how in [\"sum\", \"ohlc\", \"prod\", \"cumsum\", \"cumprod\"]:\n                # Avoid overflow during group op\n                if values.dtype.kind == \"i\":\n                    values = ensure_int64(values)\n                else:\n                    values = ensure_uint64(values)\n\n        return values\n\n    def _get_output_shape(self, ngroups: int, values: np.ndarray) -> Shape:\n        how = self.how\n        kind = self.kind\n\n        arity = self._cython_arity.get(how, 1)\n\n        out_shape: Shape\n        if how == \"ohlc\":\n            out_shape = (ngroups, arity)\n        elif arity > 1:\n            raise NotImplementedError(\n                \"arity of more than 1 is not supported for the 'how' argument\"\n            )\n        elif kind == \"transform\":\n            out_shape = values.shape\n        else:\n            out_shape = (ngroups, *values.shape[1:])\n        return out_shape\n\n    def _get_out_dtype(self, dtype: np.dtype) -> np.dtype:\n        how = self.how\n\n        if how == \"rank\":\n            out_dtype = \"float64\"\n        elif how in [\"idxmin\", \"idxmax\"]:\n            # The Cython implementation only produces the row number; we'll take\n            # from the index using this in post processing\n            out_dtype = \"intp\"\n        elif dtype.kind in \"iufcb\":\n            out_dtype = f\"{dtype.kind}{dtype.itemsize}\"\n        else:\n            out_dtype = \"object\"\n        return np.dtype(out_dtype)\n\n    def _get_result_dtype(self, dtype: np.dtype) -> np.dtype:\n        \"\"\"\n        Get the desired dtype of a result based on the\n        input dtype and how it was computed.\n\n        Parameters\n        ----------\n        dtype : np.dtype\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        np.dtype\n            The desired dtype of the result.\n        \"\"\"\n        how = self.how\n\n        if how in [\"sum\", \"cumsum\", \"sum\", \"prod\", \"cumprod\"]:\n            if dtype == np.dtype(bool):\n                return np.dtype(np.int64)\n        elif how in [\"mean\", \"median\", \"var\", \"std\", \"sem\"]:\n            if dtype.kind in \"fc\":\n                return dtype\n            elif dtype.kind in \"iub\":\n                return np.dtype(np.float64)\n        return dtype\n\n    @final\n    def _cython_op_ndim_compat(\n        self,\n        values: np.ndarray,\n        *,\n        min_count: int,\n        ngroups: int,\n        comp_ids: np.ndarray,\n        mask: npt.NDArray[np.bool_] | None = None,\n        result_mask: npt.NDArray[np.bool_] | None = None,\n        initial: Any = 0,\n        **kwargs,\n    ) -> np.ndarray:\n        if values.ndim == 1:\n            # expand to 2d, dispatch, then squeeze if appropriate\n            values2d = values[None, :]\n            if mask is not None:\n                mask = mask[None, :]\n            if result_mask is not None:\n                result_mask = result_mask[None, :]\n            res = self._call_cython_op(\n                values2d,\n                min_count=min_count,\n                ngroups=ngroups,\n                comp_ids=comp_ids,\n                mask=mask,\n                result_mask=result_mask,\n                initial=initial,\n                **kwargs,\n            )\n            if res.shape[0] == 1:\n                return res[0]\n\n            # otherwise we have OHLC\n            return res.T\n\n        return self._call_cython_op(\n            values,\n            min_count=min_count,\n            ngroups=ngroups,\n            comp_ids=comp_ids,\n            mask=mask,\n            result_mask=result_mask,\n            initial=initial,\n            **kwargs,\n        )\n\n    @final\n    def _call_cython_op(\n        self,\n        values: np.ndarray,  # np.ndarray[ndim=2]\n        *,\n        min_count: int,\n        ngroups: int,\n        comp_ids: np.ndarray,\n        mask: npt.NDArray[np.bool_] | None,\n        result_mask: npt.NDArray[np.bool_] | None,\n        initial: Any = 0,\n        **kwargs,\n    ) -> np.ndarray:  # np.ndarray[ndim=2]\n        orig_values = values\n\n        dtype = values.dtype\n        is_numeric = dtype.kind in \"iufcb\"\n\n        is_datetimelike = dtype.kind in \"mM\"\n\n        if self.how in [\"any\", \"all\"]:\n            if mask is None:\n                mask = isna(values)\n\n        if is_datetimelike:\n            values = values.view(\"int64\")\n            is_numeric = True\n        elif dtype.kind == \"b\":\n            values = values.view(\"uint8\")\n        if values.dtype == \"float16\":\n            values = values.astype(np.float32)\n\n        if self.how in [\"any\", \"all\"]:\n            if dtype == object:\n                if kwargs[\"skipna\"]:\n                    # GH#37501: don't raise on pd.NA when skipna=True\n                    if mask is not None and mask.any():\n                        # mask on original values computed separately\n                        values = values.copy()\n                        values[mask] = True\n            values = values.astype(bool, copy=False).view(np.int8)\n            is_numeric = True\n\n        values = values.T\n        if mask is not None:\n            mask = mask.T\n            if result_mask is not None:\n                result_mask = result_mask.T\n\n        out_shape = self._get_output_shape(ngroups, values)\n        func = self._get_cython_function(self.kind, self.how, values.dtype, is_numeric)\n        values = self._get_cython_vals(values)\n        out_dtype = self._get_out_dtype(values.dtype)\n\n        result = maybe_fill(np.empty(out_shape, dtype=out_dtype))\n        if self.kind == \"aggregate\":\n            counts = np.zeros(ngroups, dtype=np.int64)\n            if self.how in [\n                \"idxmin\",\n                \"idxmax\",\n                \"min\",\n                \"max\",\n                \"mean\",\n                \"last\",\n                \"first\",\n                \"sum\",\n                \"median\",\n            ]:\n                if self.how == \"sum\":\n                    # pass in through kwargs only for sum (other functions don't have\n                    # the keyword)\n                    kwargs[\"initial\"] = initial\n                func(\n                    out=result,\n                    counts=counts,\n                    values=values,\n                    labels=comp_ids,\n                    min_count=min_count,\n                    mask=mask,\n                    result_mask=result_mask,\n                    is_datetimelike=is_datetimelike,\n                    **kwargs,\n                )\n            elif self.how in [\"sem\", \"std\", \"var\", \"ohlc\", \"prod\"]:\n                if self.how in [\"std\", \"sem\"]:\n                    kwargs[\"is_datetimelike\"] = is_datetimelike\n                func(\n                    result,\n                    counts,\n                    values,\n                    comp_ids,\n                    min_count=min_count,\n                    mask=mask,\n                    result_mask=result_mask,\n                    **kwargs,\n                )\n            elif self.how in [\"any\", \"all\"]:\n                func(\n                    out=result,\n                    values=values,\n                    labels=comp_ids,\n                    mask=mask,\n                    result_mask=result_mask,\n                    **kwargs,\n                )\n                result = result.astype(bool, copy=False)\n            elif self.how in [\"skew\", \"kurt\"]:\n                func(\n                    out=result,\n                    counts=counts,\n                    values=values,\n                    labels=comp_ids,\n                    mask=mask,\n                    result_mask=result_mask,\n                    **kwargs,\n                )\n                if dtype == object:\n                    result = result.astype(object)\n\n            else:\n                raise NotImplementedError(f\"{self.how} is not implemented\")\n        else:\n            # TODO: min_count\n            if self.how != \"rank\":\n                # TODO: should rank take result_mask?\n                kwargs[\"result_mask\"] = result_mask\n            func(\n                out=result,\n                values=values,\n                labels=comp_ids,\n                ngroups=ngroups,\n                is_datetimelike=is_datetimelike,\n                mask=mask,\n                **kwargs,\n            )\n\n        if self.kind == \"aggregate\" and self.how not in [\"idxmin\", \"idxmax\"]:\n            # i.e. counts is defined.  Locations where count<min_count\n            # need to have the result set to np.nan, which may require casting,\n            # see GH#40767. For idxmin/idxmax is handled specially via post-processing\n            if result.dtype.kind in \"iu\" and not is_datetimelike:\n                # if the op keeps the int dtypes, we have to use 0\n                cutoff = max(0 if self.how in [\"sum\", \"prod\"] else 1, min_count)\n                empty_groups = counts < cutoff\n                if empty_groups.any():\n                    if result_mask is not None:\n                        assert result_mask[empty_groups].all()\n                    else:\n                        # Note: this conversion could be lossy, see GH#40767\n                        result = result.astype(\"float64\")\n                        result[empty_groups] = np.nan\n\n        result = result.T\n\n        if self.how not in self.cast_blocklist:\n            # e.g. if we are int64 and need to restore to datetime64/timedelta64\n            # \"rank\" is the only member of cast_blocklist we get here\n            # Casting only needed for float16, bool, datetimelike,\n            #  and self.how in [\"sum\", \"prod\", \"ohlc\", \"cumprod\"]\n            res_dtype = self._get_result_dtype(orig_values.dtype)\n            op_result = maybe_downcast_to_dtype(result, res_dtype)\n        else:\n            op_result = result\n\n        return op_result\n\n    @final\n    def _validate_axis(self, axis: AxisInt, values: ArrayLike) -> None:\n        if values.ndim > 2:\n            raise NotImplementedError(\"number of dimensions is currently limited to 2\")\n        if values.ndim == 2:\n            assert axis == 1, axis\n        elif not is_1d_only_ea_dtype(values.dtype):\n            # Note: it is *not* the case that axis is always 0 for 1-dim values,\n            #  as we can have 1D ExtensionArrays that we need to treat as 2D\n            assert axis == 0\n\n    @final\n    def cython_operation(\n        self,\n        *,\n        values: ArrayLike,\n        axis: AxisInt,\n        min_count: int = -1,\n        comp_ids: np.ndarray,\n        ngroups: int,\n        **kwargs,\n    ) -> ArrayLike:\n        \"\"\"\n        Call our cython function, with appropriate pre- and post- processing.\n        \"\"\"\n        self._validate_axis(axis, values)\n\n        if not isinstance(values, np.ndarray):\n            # i.e. ExtensionArray\n            return values._groupby_op(\n                how=self.how,\n                has_dropped_na=self.has_dropped_na,\n                min_count=min_count,\n                ngroups=ngroups,\n                ids=comp_ids,\n                **kwargs,\n            )\n\n        return self._cython_op_ndim_compat(\n            values,\n            min_count=min_count,\n            ngroups=ngroups,\n            comp_ids=comp_ids,\n            mask=None,\n            **kwargs,\n        )\n\n\nclass BaseGrouper:\n    \"\"\"\n    This is an internal Grouper class, which actually holds\n    the generated groups\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    axis : Index\n    groupings : Sequence[Grouping]\n        all the grouping instances to handle in this grouper\n        for example for grouper list to groupby, need to pass the list\n    sort : bool, default True\n        whether this grouper will give sorted result or not\n\n    \"\"\"\n\n    axis: Index\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        axis: Index,\n        groupings: list[grouper.Grouping],\n        sort: bool = True,\n        dropna: bool = True,\n    ) -> None:\n        assert isinstance(axis, Index), axis\n\n        self.axis = axis\n        self._groupings = groupings\n        self._sort = sort\n        self.dropna = dropna\n\n    @property\n    def groupings(self) -> list[grouper.Grouping]:\n        return self._groupings\n\n    def __iter__(self) -> Iterator[Hashable]:\n        return iter(self.indices)\n\n    @property\n    def nkeys(self) -> int:\n        return len(self.groupings)\n\n    def get_iterator(self, data: NDFrameT) -> Iterator[tuple[Hashable, NDFrameT]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Groupby iterator\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        Generator yielding sequence of (name, subsetted object)\n        for each group\n        \"\"\"\n        splitter = self._get_splitter(data)\n        # TODO: Would be more efficient to skip unobserved for transforms\n        keys = self.result_index\n        yield from zip(keys, splitter, strict=True)\n\n    @final\n    def _get_splitter(self, data: NDFrame) -> DataSplitter:\n        \"\"\"\n        Returns\n        -------\n        Generator yielding subsetted objects\n        \"\"\"\n        if isinstance(data, Series):\n            klass: type[DataSplitter] = SeriesSplitter\n        else:\n            # i.e. DataFrame\n            klass = FrameSplitter\n\n        return klass(\n            data,\n            self.ngroups,\n            sorted_ids=self._sorted_ids,\n            sort_idx=self.result_ilocs,\n        )\n\n    @cache_readonly\n    def indices(self) -> dict[Hashable, npt.NDArray[np.intp]]:\n        \"\"\"dict {group name -> group indices}\"\"\"\n        if len(self.groupings) == 1 and isinstance(self.result_index, CategoricalIndex):\n            # This shows unused categories in indices GH#38642\n            result = self.groupings[0].indices\n        else:\n            codes_list = [ping.codes for ping in self.groupings]\n            result = get_indexer_dict(codes_list, self.levels)\n        if not self.dropna:\n            has_mi = isinstance(self.result_index, MultiIndex)\n            if not has_mi and self.result_index.hasnans:\n                result = {\n                    np.nan if isna(key) else key: value for key, value in result.items()\n                }\n            elif has_mi:\n                # MultiIndex has no efficient way to tell if there are NAs\n                result = {\n                    # error: \"Hashable\" has no attribute \"__iter__\" (not iterable)\n                    tuple(np.nan if isna(comp) else comp for comp in key): value  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n                    for key, value in result.items()\n                }\n\n        return result\n\n    @final\n    @cache_readonly\n    def result_ilocs(self) -> npt.NDArray[np.intp]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Get the original integer locations of result_index in the input.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Original indices are where group_index would go via sorting.\n        # But when dropna is true, we need to remove null values while accounting for\n        # any gaps that then occur because of them.\n        ids = self.ids\n\n        if self.has_dropped_na:\n            mask = np.where(ids >= 0)\n            # Count how many gaps are caused by previous null values for each position\n            null_gaps = np.cumsum(ids == -1)[mask]\n            ids = ids[mask]\n\n        result = get_group_index_sorter(ids, self.ngroups)\n\n        if self.has_dropped_na:\n            # Shift by the number of prior null gaps\n            result += np.take(null_gaps, result)\n\n        return result\n\n    @property\n    def codes(self) -> list[npt.NDArray[np.signedinteger]]:\n        return [ping.codes for ping in self.groupings]\n\n    @property\n    def levels(self) -> list[Index]:\n        if len(self.groupings) > 1:\n            # mypy doesn't know result_index must be a MultiIndex\n            return list(self.result_index.levels)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        else:\n            return [self.result_index]\n\n    @property\n    def names(self) -> list[Hashable]:\n        return [ping.name for ping in self.groupings]\n\n    @final\n    def size(self) -> Series:\n        \"\"\"\n        Compute group sizes.\n        \"\"\"\n        ids = self.ids\n        ngroups = self.ngroups\n        out: np.ndarray | list\n        if ngroups:\n            out = np.bincount(ids[ids != -1], minlength=ngroups)\n        else:\n            out = []\n        return Series(out, index=self.result_index, dtype=\"int64\", copy=False)\n\n    @cache_readonly\n    def groups(self) -> dict[Hashable, Index]:\n        \"\"\"dict {group name -> group labels}\"\"\"\n        if len(self.groupings) == 1:\n            return self.groupings[0].groups\n        result_index, ids = self.result_index_and_ids\n        values = result_index._values\n        categories = Categorical.from_codes(ids, categories=range(len(result_index)))\n        result = {\n            # mypy is not aware that group has to be an integer\n            values[group]: self.axis.take(axis_ilocs)  # type: ignore[call-overload]\n            for group, axis_ilocs in categories._reverse_indexer().items()\n        }\n        return result\n\n    @final\n    @cache_readonly\n    def is_monotonic(self) -> bool:\n        # return if my group orderings are monotonic\n        return Index(self.ids, copy=False).is_monotonic_increasing\n\n    @final\n    @cache_readonly\n    def has_dropped_na(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Whether grouper has null value(s) that are dropped.\n        \"\"\"\n        return bool((self.ids < 0).any())\n\n    @cache_readonly\n    def codes_info(self) -> npt.NDArray[np.intp]:\n        # return the codes of items in original grouped axis\n        return self.ids\n\n    @final\n    @cache_readonly\n    def ngroups(self) -> int:\n        return len(self.result_index)\n\n    @property\n    def result_index(self) -> Index:\n        return self.result_index_and_ids[0]\n\n    @property\n    def ids(self) -> npt.NDArray[np.intp]:\n        return self.result_index_and_ids[1]\n\n    @cache_readonly\n    def result_index_and_ids(self) -> tuple[Index, npt.NDArray[np.intp]]:\n        levels = [\n            Index._with_infer(ping.uniques, copy=False) for ping in self.groupings\n        ]\n        obs = [\n            ping._observed or not ping._passed_categorical for ping in self.groupings\n        ]\n        sorts = [ping._sort for ping in self.groupings]\n        # When passed a categorical grouping, keep all categories\n        for k, (ping, level) in enumerate(zip(self.groupings, levels, strict=True)):\n            if ping._passed_categorical:\n                levels[k] = level.set_categories(ping._orig_cats)\n\n        if len(self.groupings) == 1:\n            result_index = levels[0]\n            result_index.name = self.names[0]\n            ids = ensure_platform_int(self.codes[0])\n        elif all(obs):\n            result_index, ids = self._ob_index_and_ids(\n                levels, self.codes, self.names, sorts\n            )\n        elif not any(obs):\n            result_index, ids = self._unob_index_and_ids(levels, self.codes, self.names)\n        else:\n            # Combine unobserved and observed parts\n            names = self.names\n            codes = [ping.codes for ping in self.groupings]\n            ob_indices = [idx for idx, ob in enumerate(obs) if ob]\n            unob_indices = [idx for idx, ob in enumerate(obs) if not ob]\n            ob_index, ob_ids = self._ob_index_and_ids(\n                levels=[levels[idx] for idx in ob_indices],\n                codes=[codes[idx] for idx in ob_indices],\n                names=[names[idx] for idx in ob_indices],\n                sorts=[sorts[idx] for idx in ob_indices],\n            )\n            unob_index, unob_ids = self._unob_index_and_ids(\n                levels=[levels[idx] for idx in unob_indices],\n                codes=[codes[idx] for idx in unob_indices],\n                names=[names[idx] for idx in unob_indices],\n            )\n\n            result_index_codes = np.concatenate(\n                [\n                    np.tile(unob_index.codes, len(ob_index)),\n                    np.repeat(ob_index.codes, len(unob_index), axis=1),\n                ],\n                axis=0,\n            )\n            _, index = np.unique(unob_indices + ob_indices, return_index=True)\n            result_index = MultiIndex(\n                levels=list(unob_index.levels) + list(ob_index.levels),\n                codes=result_index_codes,\n                names=list(unob_index.names) + list(ob_index.names),\n            ).reorder_levels(index)\n\n            # The sum here will get -1 values wrong when dropna=True;\n            # we will fix at the end.\n            ids = len(unob_index) * ob_ids + unob_ids\n\n            if any(sorts):\n                # Sort result_index and recode ids using the new order\n                n_levels = len(sorts)\n                drop_levels = [\n                    n_levels - idx\n                    for idx, sort in enumerate(reversed(sorts), 1)\n                    if not sort\n                ]\n                if len(drop_levels) > 0:\n                    sorter = result_index._drop_level_numbers(drop_levels).argsort()\n                else:\n                    sorter = result_index.argsort()\n                result_index = result_index.take(sorter)\n                _, index = np.unique(sorter, return_index=True)\n                ids = ensure_platform_int(ids)\n                ids = index.take(ids)\n            else:\n                # Recode ids and reorder result_index with observed groups up front,\n                # unobserved at the end\n                ids, uniques = compress_group_index(ids, sort=False)\n                ids = ensure_platform_int(ids)\n                taker = np.concatenate(\n                    [uniques, np.delete(np.arange(len(result_index)), uniques)]\n                )\n                result_index = result_index.take(taker)\n\n            if self.dropna:\n                ids = np.where((ob_ids < 0) | (unob_ids < 0), -1, ids)\n\n        return result_index, ids\n\n    @property\n    def observed_grouper(self) -> BaseGrouper:\n        if all(ping._observed for ping in self.groupings):\n            return self\n\n        return self._observed_grouper\n\n    @cache_readonly\n    def _observed_grouper(self) -> BaseGrouper:\n        groupings = [ping.observed_grouping for ping in self.groupings]\n        grouper = BaseGrouper(self.axis, groupings, sort=self._sort, dropna=self.dropna)\n        return grouper\n\n    def _ob_index_and_ids(\n        self,\n        levels: list[Index],\n        codes: list[npt.NDArray[np.intp]],\n        names: list[Hashable],\n        sorts: list[bool],\n    ) -> tuple[MultiIndex, npt.NDArray[np.intp]]:\n        consistent_sorting = all(sorts[0] == sort for sort in sorts[1:])\n        sort_in_compress = sorts[0] if consistent_sorting else False\n        shape = tuple(len(level) for level in levels)\n        group_index = get_group_index(codes, shape, sort=True, xnull=True)\n        ob_ids, obs_group_ids = compress_group_index(group_index, sort=sort_in_compress)\n        ob_ids = ensure_platform_int(ob_ids)\n        ob_index_codes = decons_obs_group_ids(\n            ob_ids, obs_group_ids, shape, codes, xnull=True\n        )\n        ob_index = MultiIndex(\n            levels=levels,\n            codes=ob_index_codes,\n            names=names,\n            verify_integrity=False,\n        )\n        if not consistent_sorting and len(ob_index) > 0:\n            # Sort by the levels where the corresponding sort argument is True\n            n_levels = len(sorts)\n            drop_levels = [\n                n_levels - idx\n                for idx, sort in enumerate(reversed(sorts), 1)\n                if not sort\n            ]\n            if len(drop_levels) > 0:\n                sorter = ob_index._drop_level_numbers(drop_levels).argsort()\n            else:\n                sorter = ob_index.argsort()\n            ob_index = ob_index.take(sorter)\n            _, index = np.unique(sorter, return_index=True)\n            ob_ids = np.where(ob_ids == -1, -1, index.take(ob_ids))\n        ob_ids = ensure_platform_int(ob_ids)\n        return ob_index, ob_ids\n\n    def _unob_index_and_ids(\n        self,\n        levels: list[Index],\n        codes: list[npt.NDArray[np.intp]],\n        names: list[Hashable],\n    ) -> tuple[MultiIndex, npt.NDArray[np.intp]]:\n        shape = tuple(len(level) for level in levels)\n        unob_ids = get_group_index(codes, shape, sort=True, xnull=True)\n        unob_index = MultiIndex.from_product(levels, names=names)\n        unob_ids = ensure_platform_int(unob_ids)\n        return unob_index, unob_ids\n\n    @final\n    def get_group_levels(self) -> Generator[Index]:\n        # Note: only called from _insert_inaxis_grouper, which\n        #  is only called for BaseGrouper, never for BinGrouper\n        result_index = self.result_index\n        if len(self.groupings) == 1:\n            yield result_index\n        else:\n            for level in range(result_index.nlevels - 1, -1, -1):\n                yield result_index.get_level_values(level)\n\n    # Note: we make this a classmethod and pass kind+how so that caching\n    #  works at the class level and not the instance level\n    @classmethod\n    @functools.cache\n    def _get_cython_function(\n        cls, kind: str, how: str, dtype: np.dtype, is_numeric: bool\n    ):\n        dtype_str = dtype.name\n        ftype = cls._CYTHON_FUNCTIONS[kind][how]\n\n        # see if there is a fused-type version of function\n        # only valid for numeric\n        if callable(ftype):\n            f = ftype\n        else:\n            f = getattr(libgroupby, ftype)\n        if is_numeric:\n            return f\n        elif dtype == np.dtype(object):\n            if how in [\"median\", \"cumprod\"]:\n                # no fused types -> no __signatures__\n                raise NotImplementedError(\n                    f\"function is not implemented for this dtype: \"\n                    f\"[how->{how},dtype->{dtype_str}]\"\n                )\n            elif how in [\"std\", \"sem\", \"idxmin\", \"idxmax\"]:\n                # We have a partial object that does not have __signatures__\n                return f\n            elif how in [\"skew\", \"kurt\"]:\n                # _get_cython_vals will convert to float64\n                pass\n            elif \"object\" not in f.__signatures__:\n                # raise NotImplementedError here rather than TypeError later\n                raise NotImplementedError(\n                    f\"function is not implemented for this dtype: \"\n                    f\"[how->{how},dtype->{dtype_str}]\"\n                )\n            return f\n        else:\n            raise NotImplementedError(\n                \"This should not be reached. Please report a bug at \"\n                \"github.com/pandas-dev/pandas/\",\n                dtype,\n            )\n\n    def _get_cython_vals(self, values: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:\n        \"\"\"\n        Cast numeric dtypes to float64 for functions that only support that.\n\n        Parameters\n        ----------\n        values : np.ndarray\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        values : np.ndarray\n        \"\"\"\n        how = self.how\n\n        if how in [\"median\", \"std\", \"sem\", \"skew\", \"kurt\"]:\n            # median only has a float64 implementation\n            # We should only get here with is_numeric, as non-numeric cases\n            #  should raise in _get_cython_function\n            values = ensure_float64(values)\n\n        elif values.dtype.kind in \"iu\":\n            if how in [\"var\", \"mean\"] or (\n                self.kind == \"transform\" and self.has_dropped_na\n            ):\n                # has_dropped_na check need for test_null_group_str_transformer\n                # result may still include NaN, so we have to cast\n                values = ensure_float64(values)\n\n            elif how in [\"sum\", \"ohlc\", \"prod\", \"cumsum\", \"cumprod\"]:\n                # Avoid overflow during group op\n                if values.dtype.kind == \"i\":\n                    values = ensure_int64(values)\n                else:\n                    values = ensure_uint64(values)\n\n        return values\n\n    def _get_output_shape(self, ngroups: int, values: np.ndarray) -> Shape:\n        how = self.how\n        kind = self.kind\n\n        arity = self._cython_arity.get(how, 1)\n\n        out_shape: Shape\n        if how == \"ohlc\":\n            out_shape = (ngroups, arity)\n        elif arity > 1:\n            raise NotImplementedError(\n                \"arity of more than 1 is not supported for the 'how' argument\"\n            )\n        elif kind == \"transform\":\n            out_shape = values.shape\n        else:\n            out_shape = (ngroups, *values.shape[1:])\n        return out_shape\n\n    def _get_out_dtype(self, dtype: np.dtype) -> np.dtype:\n        how = self.how\n\n        if how == \"rank\":\n            out_dtype = \"float64\"\n        elif how in [\"idxmin\", \"idxmax\"]:\n            # The Cython implementation only produces the row number; we'll take\n            # from the index using this in post processing\n            out_dtype = \"intp\"\n        elif dtype.kind in \"iufcb\":\n            out_dtype = f\"{dtype.kind}{dtype.itemsize}\"\n        else:\n            out_dtype = \"object\"\n        return np.dtype(out_dtype)\n\n    def _get_result_dtype(self, dtype: np.dtype) -> np.dtype:\n        \"\"\"\n        Get the desired dtype of a result based on the\n        input dtype and how it was computed.\n\n        Parameters\n        ----------\n        dtype : np.dtype\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        np.dtype\n            The desired dtype of the result.\n        \"\"\"\n        how = self.how\n\n        if how in [\"sum\", \"cumsum\", \"sum\", \"prod\", \"cumprod\"]:\n            if dtype == np.dtype(bool):\n                return np.dtype(np.int64)\n        elif how in [\"mean\", \"median\", \"var\", \"std\", \"sem\"]:\n            if dtype.kind in \"fc\":\n                return dtype\n            elif dtype.kind in \"iub\":\n                return np.dtype(np.float64)\n        return dtype\n\n    @final\n    def _cython_op_ndim_compat(\n        self,\n        values: np.ndarray,\n        *,\n        min_count: int,\n        ngroups: int,\n        comp_ids: np.ndarray,\n        mask: npt.NDArray[np.bool_] | None = None,\n        result_mask: npt.NDArray[np.bool_] | None = None,\n        initial: Any = 0,\n        **kwargs,\n    ) -> np.ndarray:\n        if values.ndim == 1:\n            # expand to 2d, dispatch, then squeeze if appropriate\n            values2d = values[None, :]\n            if mask is not None:\n                mask = mask[None, :]\n            if result_mask is not None:\n                result_mask = result_mask[None, :]\n            res = self._call_cython_op(\n                values2d,\n                min_count=min_count,\n                ngroups=ngroups,\n                comp_ids=comp_ids,\n                mask=mask,\n                result_mask=result_mask,\n                initial=initial,\n                **kwargs,\n            )\n            if res.shape[0] == 1:\n                return res[0]\n\n            # otherwise we have OHLC\n            return res.T\n\n        return self._call_cython_op(\n            values,\n            min_count=min_count,\n            ngroups=ngroups,\n            comp_ids=comp_ids,\n            mask=mask,\n            result_mask=result_mask,\n            initial=initial,\n            **kwargs,\n        )\n\n    @final\n    def _call_cython_op(\n        self,\n        values: np.ndarray,  # np.ndarray[ndim=2]\n        *,\n        min_count: int,\n        ngroups: int,\n        comp_ids: np.ndarray,\n        mask: npt.NDArray[np.bool_] | None,\n        result_mask: npt.NDArray[np.bool_] | None,\n        initial: Any = 0,\n        **kwargs,\n    ) -> np.ndarray:  # np.ndarray[ndim=2]\n        orig_values = values\n\n        dtype = values.dtype\n        is_numeric = dtype.kind in \"iufcb\"\n\n        is_datetimelike = dtype.kind in \"mM\"\n\n        if self.how in [\"any\", \"all\"]:\n            if mask is None:\n                mask = isna(values)\n\n        if is_datetimelike:\n            values = values.view(\"int64\")\n            is_numeric = True\n        elif dtype.kind == \"b\":\n            values = values.view(\"uint8\")\n        if values.dtype == \"float16\":\n            values = values.astype(np.float32)\n\n        if self.how in [\"any\", \"all\"]:\n            if dtype == object:\n                if kwargs[\"skipna\"]:\n                    # GH#37501: don't raise on pd.NA when skipna=True\n                    if mask is not None and mask.any():\n                        # mask on original values computed separately\n                        values = values.copy()\n                        values[mask] = True\n            values = values.astype(bool, copy=False).view(np.int8)\n            is_numeric = True\n\n        values = values.T\n        if mask is not None:\n            mask = mask.T\n            if result_mask is not None:\n                result_mask = result_mask.T\n\n        out_shape = self._get_output_shape(ngroups, values)\n        func = self._get_cython_function(self.kind, self.how, values.dtype, is_numeric)\n        values = self._get_cython_vals(values)\n        out_dtype = self._get_out_dtype(values.dtype)\n\n        result = maybe_fill(np.empty(out_shape, dtype=out_dtype))\n        if self.kind == \"aggregate\":\n            counts = np.zeros(ngroups, dtype=np.int64)\n            if self.how in [\n                \"idxmin\",\n                \"idxmax\",\n                \"min\",\n                \"max\",\n                \"mean\",\n                \"last\",\n                \"first\",\n                \"sum\",\n                \"median\",\n            ]:\n                if self.how == \"sum\":\n                    # pass in through kwargs only for sum (other functions don't have\n                    # the keyword)\n                    kwargs[\"initial\"] = initial\n                func(\n                    out=result,\n                    counts=counts,\n                    values=values,\n                    labels=comp_ids,\n                    min_count=min_count,\n                    mask=mask,\n                    result_mask=result_mask,\n                    is_datetimelike=is_datetimelike,\n                    **kwargs,\n                )\n            elif self.how in [\"sem\", \"std\", \"var\", \"ohlc\", \"prod\"]:\n                if self.how in [\"std\", \"sem\"]:\n                    kwargs[\"is_datetimelike\"] = is_datetimelike\n                func(\n                    result,\n                    counts,\n                    values,\n                    comp_ids,\n                    min_count=min_count,\n                    mask=mask,\n                    result_mask=result_mask,\n                    **kwargs,\n                )\n            elif self.how in [\"any\", \"all\"]:\n                func(\n                    out=result,\n                    values=values,\n                    labels=comp_ids,\n                    mask=mask,\n                    result_mask=result_mask,\n                    **kwargs,\n                )\n                result = result.astype(bool, copy=False)\n            elif self.how in [\"skew\", \"kurt\"]:\n                func(\n                    out=result,\n                    counts=counts,\n                    values=values,\n                    labels=comp_ids,\n                    mask=mask,\n                    result_mask=result_mask,\n                    **kwargs,\n                )\n                if dtype == object:\n                    result = result.astype(object)\n\n            else:\n                raise NotImplementedError(f\"{self.how} is not implemented\")\n        else:\n            # TODO: min_count\n            if self.how != \"rank\":\n                # TODO: should rank take result_mask?\n                kwargs[\"result_mask\"] = result_mask\n            func(\n                out=result,\n                values=values,\n                labels=comp_ids,\n                ngroups=ngroups,\n                is_datetimelike=is_datetimelike,\n                mask=mask,\n                **kwargs,\n            )\n\n        if self.kind == \"aggregate\" and self.how not in [\"idxmin\", \"idxmax\"]:\n            # i.e. counts is defined.  Locations where count<min_count\n            # need to have the result set to np.nan, which may require casting,\n            # see GH#40767. For idxmin/idxmax is handled specially via post-processing\n            if result.dtype.kind in \"iu\" and not is_datetimelike:\n                # if the op keeps the int dtypes, we have to use 0\n                cutoff = max(0 if self.how in [\"sum\", \"prod\"] else 1, min_count)\n                empty_groups = counts < cutoff\n                if empty_groups.any():\n                    if result_mask is not None:\n                        assert result_mask[empty_groups].all()\n                    else:\n                        # Note: this conversion could be lossy, see GH#40767\n                        result = result.astype(\"float64\")\n                        result[empty_groups] = np.nan\n\n        result = result.T\n\n        if self.how not in self.cast_blocklist:\n            # e.g. if we are int64 and need to restore to datetime64/timedelta64\n            # \"rank\" is the only member of cast_blocklist we get here\n            # Casting only needed for float16, bool, datetimelike,\n            #  and self.how in [\"sum\", \"prod\", \"ohlc\", \"cumprod\"]\n            res_dtype = self._get_result_dtype(orig_values.dtype)\n            op_result = maybe_downcast_to_dtype(result, res_dtype)\n        else:\n            op_result = result\n\n        return op_result\n\n    @final\n    def _validate_axis(self, axis: AxisInt, values: ArrayLike) -> **kwargs,\n        )\n\n\nclass BaseGrouper:\n    \"\"\"\n    This is an internal Grouper class, which actually holds\n    the generated groups\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    axis : Index\n @final\n    def _get_splitter(self, data: NDFrame) -> DataSplitter:\n        \"\"\"\n        Returns\n        -------\n        Generator yielding subsetted objects\n        \"\"\"\n        if data,\n            self.ngroups,\n            sorted_ids=self._sorted_ids,\n            sort_idx=self.result_ilocs,\n        )\n\n    @cache_readonly\n    def indices(self) -> dict[Hashable, npt.NDArray[np.intp]]:\n        \"\"\"dict {group name -> group indices}\"\"\"\n        if len(self.groupings) == 1 and isinstance(self.result_index, CategoricalIndex):\n            # This shows unused categories in indices GH#38642\n            result = self.groupings[0].indices\n        else:\n            codes_list = [ping.codes for ping in self.groupings]\n            result = @cache_readonly\n    def result_ilocs(self) -> npt.NDArray[np.intp]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Get the original integer locations of result_index in the input.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Original indices are where group_index would go via sorting.\n        # But when dropna is true, we need to remove null values while accounting for\n        # any gaps that then occur because of them.\n        ids = self.ids\n\n        if self.has_dropped_na:\n            mask = np.where(ids >= 0)\n            # Count how many gaps are caused by previous null values for each position\n            null_gaps = np.cumsum(ids == -1)[mask]\n            ids = ids[mask]\n\n        result = get_group_index_sorter(ids, self.ngroups)\n\n        if self.has_dropped_na:\n            # Shift by the number of prior out: np.ndarray | list\n        if ngroups:\n            out = np.bincount(ids[ids != -1], minlength=ngroups)\n        else:\n            out = []\n        return Series(out, index=self.result_index, copy=False) for ping in self.groupings\n        ]\n        obs = [\n            ping._observed or not ping._passed_categorical for ping in self.groupings\n        ]\n        sorts = [ping._sort for ping in self.groupings]\n        # When passed a categorical grouping, keep all categories\n        for k, (ping, level) in enumerate(zip(self.groupings, levels, strict=True)):\n            if ping._passed_categorical:\n                levels[k] = level.set_categories(ping._orig_cats)\n\n        if len(self.groupings) == 1:\n            result_index = levels[0]\n            result_index.name = self.names[0]\n            ids = ensure_platform_int(self.codes[0])\n        elif all(obs):\n            result_index, ids = self._ob_index_and_ids(\n                levels, self.codes, self.names, sorts\n            )\n        elif not any(obs):\n            result_index, ids = self._unob_index_and_ids(levels, self.codes, self.names)\n        else:\n            # Combine unobserved and observed parts\n            names = self.names\n            codes = [ping.codes for ping in self.groupings]\n            ob_indices = [idx for idx, ob in enumerate(obs) if ob]\n            unob_indices = [idx for idx, ob in enumerate(obs) if not ob]\n            ob_index, ob_ids = self._ob_index_and_ids(\n                levels=[levels[idx] for idx in ob_indices],\n                codes=[codes[idx] for idx in ob_indices],\n                names=[names[idx] for idx in ob_indices],\n                sorts=[sorts[idx] for idx in ob_indices],\n            )\n            unob_index, np.repeat(ob_index.codes, len(unob_index), axis=1),\n                ],\n                axis=0,\n            )\n            _, index = np.unique(unob_indices + ob_indices, return_index=True)\n            result_index = MultiIndex(\n                levels=list(unob_index.levels) + list(ob_index.levels),\n                codes=result_index_codes,\n                names=list(unob_index.names) + drop_levels = [\n                    n_levels - idx\n                    for idx, sort in enumerate(reversed(sorts), 1)\n                    if not sort\n                ]\n                if result_index = result_index.take(sorter)\n                _, index = np.unique(sorter, return_index=True)\n                ids = ensure_platform_int(ids)\n                ids = index.take(ids)\n            else:\n                # Recode ids and reorder result_index with observed groups up front,\n                # unobserved at the end\n                ids, uniques = compress_group_index(ids, )\n                result_index = result_index.take(taker)\n\n            if self.dropna:\n                ids = np.where((ob_ids < 0) | (unob_ids < 0), -1, ids)\n\n        return result_index, Leverages khash-like behavior through\n+        cached index computations.\n+        \"\"\"\n+        result = np.empty(self.ngroups, dtype=\"O\")\n+\n+        if self.ngroups == 0:\n+            return result\n+\n+        # Slice arrays directly without going through Series machinery\n+            if start < end:\n+                # Direct array slicing is faster than iloc\n+                sliced_array = sorted_array[start:end]\n+                sliced_index = sorted_index[start:end]\n+            else:\n+                # Empty group case\n+                sliced_array = sorted_array[0:0]\n+                sliced_index = sorted_index[0:0]\n+\n+            # Create Series directly with sliced data (faster than iloc)\n+            group_series = obj._constructor(\n+                sliced_array,\n+                index=sliced_index,\n+                name=obj.name,\n+                dtype=obj.dtype,\n+            )\n+\n+            res = func(group_series)\n+            res = extract_result(res)\n+\n+            if not initialized:\n+                # We only do this validation on the first iteration\n+                check_result_array(res, obj.dtype)\n+                initialized = True\n+\n+            result[group_id] = res\n+\n+        return result\n+\n     @final\n     def apply_groupwise(\n         self, f: Callable, data: DataFrame | Series","stderr":"","interrupted":false,"isImage":false,"noOutputExpected":false}}
